Notes: Columns provide, country code, race date, race venue, number of runnings, numbers of male+female finishers (or total if male/female not known), race name, men's winner, and women's winner. Ages and nationalities are given when known. Ages may be based on year of birth. A time with "xx" means the seconds are not known or were not recorded. An "x" appended to the time means the mark is not statistically valid (short course or excessively downhill or excessively wind-aided). An "a" appended to the time means the mark is statistically valid but the course is point-to-point or otherwise not record-quality. A "t" appended to the time indicates this was a tie.
